        title: 'Documentaci√≥n API REST',
        content: `# API REST - NEXUS AI Studio

## Descripci√≥n
API RESTful para la gesti√≥n de proyectos y archivos en NEXUS AI Studio.

## Base URL
\`\`\`
https://api.nexus-ai.studio/v1
\`\`\`

## Autenticaci√≥n
Todas las peticiones requieren un token de autenticaci√≥n en el header:
\`\`\`
Authorization: Bearer <token>
\`\`\`

## Endpoints

### Proyectos

#### GET /projects
Obtiene la lista de proyectos del usuario.

**Respuesta:**
\`\`\`json
{
  "projects": [
    {
      "id": "proj_123",
      "name": "Mi Proyecto",
      "description": "Descripci√≥n del proyecto",
      "created_at": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z",
      "updated_at": "2024-01-15T15:45:00Z",
      "files_count": 25,
      "size": 1048576
    }
  ],
  "total": 1,
  "page": 1,
  "limit": 20
}
\`\`\`

#### POST /projects
Crea un nuevo proyecto.

**Body:**
\`\`\`json
{
  "name": "Nuevo Proyecto",
  "description": "Descripci√≥n opcional",
  "template": "react" // opcional
}
\`\`\`

#### GET /projects/{id}
Obtiene los detalles de un proyecto espec√≠fico.

#### PUT /projects/{id}
Actualiza un proyecto existente.

#### DELETE /projects/{id}
Elimina un proyecto.

### Archivos

#### GET /projects/{project_id}/files
Obtiene la lista de archivos de un proyecto.

#### POST /projects/{project_id}/files
Crea un nuevo archivo en el proyecto.

#### GET /files/{id}
Obtiene el contenido de un archivo.

#### PUT /files/{id}
Actualiza el contenido de un archivo.

#### DELETE /files/{id}
Elimina un archivo.

### IA

#### POST /ai/chat
Env√≠a un mensaje al modelo de IA.

**Body:**
\`\`\`json
{
  "message": "Genera una funci√≥n en Python",
  "model": "gpt-4",
  "context": {
    "project_id": "proj_123",
    "file_id": "file_456"
  }
}
\`\`\`

#### POST /ai/analyze
Analiza c√≥digo o archivos.

#### POST /ai/generate
Genera c√≥digo o contenido.

## C√≥digos de Estado

- \`200\` - OK
- \`201\` - Created
- \`400\` - Bad Request
- \`401\` - Unauthorized
- \`403\` - Forbidden
- \`404\` - Not Found
- \`429\` - Too Many Requests
- \`500\` - Internal Server Error

## L√≠mites de Uso

- M√°ximo 1000 peticiones por hora
- Tama√±o m√°ximo de archivo: 10MB
- M√°ximo 100 proyectos por usuario

## Ejemplos de Uso

### Crear un proyecto
\`\`\`bash
curl -X POST https://api.nexus-ai.studio/v1/projects \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer <token>" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{
    "name": "Mi App React",
    "description": "Aplicaci√≥n web con React",
    "template": "react"
  }'
\`\`\`

### Enviar mensaje a IA
\`\`\`bash
curl -X POST https://api.nexus-ai.studio/v1/ai/chat \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer <token>" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{
    "message": "Crea un componente React para login",
    "model": "gpt-4"
  }'
\`\`\``,
        metadata: {
          model: 'GPT-4',
          timestamp: new Date(Date.now() - 7200000),
          tokens: 890,
          size: 4567,
          description: 'Documentaci√≥n completa de la API REST',
          tags: ['api', 'documentation', 'rest', 'endpoints'],
          version: 1
        },
        executable: false,
        editable: true
      }
    ];
    
    setArtifacts(sampleArtifacts);
    if (sampleArtifacts.length > 0) {
      setSelectedArtifact(sampleArtifacts[0]);
    }
  }, []);

  const getArtifactIcon = (type: string) => {
    switch (type) {
      case 'code': return CodeBracketIcon;
      case 'html': return GlobeAltIcon;
      case 'text': return DocumentTextIcon;
      case 'image': return PhotoIcon;
      case 'video': return VideoCameraIcon;
      case 'audio': return MusicalNoteIcon;
      case 'component': return CodeBracketIcon;
      default: return DocumentTextIcon;
    }
  };

  const executeArtifact = async () => {
    if (!selectedArtifact || !selectedArtifact.executable) return;
    
    setIsExecuting(true);
    try {
      if (selectedArtifact.type === 'html') {
        // Ejecutar HTML en iframe
        if (previewRef.current) {
          const doc = previewRef.current.contentDocument;
          if (doc) {
            doc.open();
            doc.write(selectedArtifact.content);
            doc.close();
          }
        }
      }
      
      setExecutionResult({ success: true, message: 'Ejecutado correctamente' });
    } catch (error) {
      setExecutionResult({ success: false, message: 'Error en la ejecuci√≥n', error });
    } finally {
      setIsExecuting(false);
    }
  };

  const saveArtifact = async () => {
    if (!selectedArtifact) return;
    
    try {
      const extension = selectedArtifact.type === 'html' ? '.html' : 
                      selectedArtifact.language === 'typescript' ? '.tsx' :
                      selectedArtifact.language === 'javascript' ? '.js' :
                      selectedArtifact.type === 'text' ? '.md' : '.txt';
      
      const fileName = `${selectedArtifact.title.replace(/\s+/g, '_')}${extension}`;
      
      await createFile(fileName, selectedArtifact.content);
      alert('Archivo guardado en el proyecto');
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error saving artifact:', error);
      alert('Error al guardar el archivo');
    }
  };

  const copyToClipboard = () => {
    if (selectedArtifact) {
      navigator.clipboard.writeText(selectedArtifact.content);
    }
  };

  const startEditing = () => {
    if (selectedArtifact) {
      setEditedContent(selectedArtifact.content);
      setIsEditing(true);
    }
  };

  const saveEdit = () => {
    if (selectedArtifact) {
      const updated = {
        ...selectedArtifact,
        content: editedContent,
        metadata: {
          ...selectedArtifact.metadata,
          version: selectedArtifact.metadata.version + 1
        }
      };
      
      setArtifacts(prev => prev.map(a => a.id === updated.id ? updated : a));
      setSelectedArtifact(updated);
      setIsEditing(false);
    }
  };

  const deleteArtifact = () => {
    if (selectedArtifact && confirm('¬øEst√°s seguro de que quieres eliminar este artefacto?')) {
      setArtifacts(prev => prev.filter(a => a.id !== selectedArtifact.id));
      const remaining = artifacts.filter(a => a.id !== selectedArtifact.id);
      setSelectedArtifact(remaining.length > 0 ? remaining[0] : null);
    }
  };

  const filteredArtifacts = artifacts.filter(artifact => {
    const matchesSearch = !searchQuery || 
      artifact.title.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
      artifact.metadata.description?.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
      artifact.metadata.tags.some(tag => tag.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()));
    
    const matchesType = selectedType === 'all' || artifact.type === selectedType;
    
    return matchesSearch && matchesType;
  });

  const navigateArtifact = (direction: 'prev' | 'next') => {
    const currentIdx = filteredArtifacts.findIndex(a => a.id === selectedArtifact?.id);
    if (currentIdx === -1) return;
    
    let newIdx;
    if (direction === 'prev') {
      newIdx = currentIdx > 0 ? currentIdx - 1 : filteredArtifacts.length - 1;
    } else {
      newIdx = currentIdx < filteredArtifacts.length - 1 ? currentIdx + 1 : 0;
    }
    
    setSelectedArtifact(filteredArtifacts[newIdx]);
    setCurrentIndex(newIdx);
  };

  const artifactTypes = [
    { id: 'all', name: 'Todos', icon: DocumentTextIcon },
    { id: 'code', name: 'C√≥digo', icon: CodeBracketIcon },
    { id: 'html', name: 'HTML', icon: GlobeAltIcon },
    { id: 'text', name: 'Texto', icon: DocumentTextIcon },
    { id: 'image', name: 'Imagen', icon: PhotoIcon },
    { id: 'video', name: 'Video', icon: VideoCameraIcon },
    { id: 'audio', name: 'Audio', icon: MusicalNoteIcon }
  ];

  return (
    <div className={`flex flex-col h-full bg-gray-800 ${className}`}>
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="p-3 border-b border-gray-700">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
          <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-200">Vista Previa de Artefactos</h3>
          <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
            <span className="text-xs text-gray-400">{artifacts.length} artefactos</span>
            {selectedArtifact && (
              <div className="flex space-x-1">
                <button
                  onClick={() => navigateArtifact('prev')}
                  className="p-1 hover:bg-gray-700 rounded"
                  title="Anterior"
                >
                  <ChevronLeftIcon className="w-4 h-4 text-gray-400" />
                </button>
                <button
                  onClick={() => navigateArtifact('next')}
                  className="p-1 hover:bg-gray-700 rounded"
                  title="Siguiente"
                >
                  <ChevronRightIcon className="w-4 h-4 text-gray-400" />
                </button>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
        
        {/* Search and filters */}
        <div className="space-y-2">
          <div className="relative">
            <MagnifyingGlassIcon className="absolute left-2 top-1/2 transform -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 text-gray-500" />
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="Buscar artefactos..."
              value={searchQuery}
              onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full pl-8 pr-3 py-1 bg-gray-700 text-white text-sm rounded border border-gray-600 focus:border-blue-500 focus:outline-none"
            />
          </div>
          
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
            {artifactTypes.map(type => (
              <button
                key={type.id}
                onClick={() => setSelectedType(type.id)}
                className={`flex items-center space-x-1 px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs transition-colors ${
                  selectedType === type.id
                    ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white'
                    : 'bg-gray-700 text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-600'
                }`}
              >
                <type.icon className="w-3 h-3" />
                <span>{type.name}</span>
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Content */}
      <div className="flex-1 flex overflow-hidden">
        {/* Artifact list */}
        <div className="w-1/3 border-r border-gray-700 overflow-y-auto">
          <div className="p-2">
            {filteredArtifacts.length === 0 ? (
              <div className="text-center text-gray-500 mt-8">
                <DocumentTextIcon className="w-12 h-12 mx-auto mb-4 opacity-50" />
                <p className="text-sm">No hay artefactos</p>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="space-y-2">
                {filteredArtifacts.map(artifact => {
                  const ArtifactIcon = getArtifactIcon(artifact.type);
                  
                  return (
                    <div
                      key={artifact.id}
                      onClick={() => setSelectedArtifact(artifact)}
                      className={`p-3 rounded-lg cursor-pointer transition-colors ${
                        selectedArtifact?.id === artifact.id
                          ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white'
                          : 'bg-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-600 text-gray-200'
                      }`}
                    >
                      <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-2">
                        <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
                          <ArtifactIcon className="w-4 h-4" />
                          <span className="text-sm font-medium">{artifact.title}</span>
                        </div>
                        <span className="text-xs opacity-75">
                          v{artifact.metadata.version}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                      
                      {artifact.metadata.description && (
                        <p className="text-xs opacity-75 line-clamp-2">
                          {artifact.metadata.description}
                        </p>
                      )}
                      
                      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mt-2">
                        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
                          {artifact.metadata.tags.slice(0, 2).map(tag => (
                            <span key={tag} className="px-1 py-0.5 bg-gray-600 text-xs rounded">
                              {tag}
                            </span>
                          ))}
                        </div>
                        <span className="text-xs opacity-75">
                          {(artifact.metadata.size / 1024).toFixed(1)}KB
                        </span>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  );
                })}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
        
        {/* Preview area */}
        <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col">
          {selectedArtifact ? (
            <>
              {/* Artifact header */}
              <div className="p-3 border-b border-gray-700">
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
                  <h4 className="text-lg font-medium text-gray-200">
                    {selectedArtifact.title}
                  </h4>
                  <div className="flex items-center space-x-1">
                    {/* View mode toggles */}
                    <div className="flex space-x-1 mr-2">
                      {[
                        { id: 'preview', icon: EyeIcon, label: 'Vista' },
                        { id: 'code', icon: CodeBracketIcon, label: 'C√≥digo' },
                        { id: 'split', icon: AdjustmentsHorizontalIcon, label: 'Split' }
                      ].map(mode => (
                        <button
                          key={mode.id}
                          onClick={() => setViewMode(mode.id as any)}
                          className={`p-1 rounded transition-colors ${
                            viewMode === mode.id
                              ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white'
                              : 'text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-200 hover:bg-gray-700'
                          }`}
                          title={mode.label}
                        >
                          <mode.icon className="w-4 h-4" />
                        </button>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                    
                    {/* Actions */}
                    <button
                      onClick={copyToClipboard}
                      className="p-1 hover:bg-gray-700 rounded"
                      title="Copiar"
                    >
                      <ClipboardDocumentIcon className="w-4 h-4 text-gray-400" />
                    </button>
                    
                    {selectedArtifact.editable && (
                      <button
                        onClick={startEditing}
                        className="p-1 hover:bg-gray-700 rounded"
                        title="Editar"
                      >
                        <PencilIcon className="w-4 h-4 text-gray-400" />
                      </button>
                    )}
                    
                    <button
                      onClick={saveArtifact}
                      className="p-1 hover:bg-gray-700 rounded"
                      title="Guardar en proyecto"
                    >
                      <ArrowDownTrayIcon className="w-4 h-4 text-gray-400" />
                    </button>
                    
                    {selectedArtifact.executable && (
                      <button
                        onClick={executeArtifact}
                        disabled={isExecuting}
                        className="p-1 hover:bg-gray-700 rounded disabled:opacity-50"
                        title="Ejecutar"
                      >
                        {isExecuting ? (
                          <ArrowPathIcon className="w-4 h-4 text-gray-400 animate-spin" />
                        ) : (
                          <PlayIcon className="w-4 h-4 text-green-400" />
                        )}
                      </button>
                    )}
                    
                    <button
                      onClick={() => setShowFullscreen(true)}
                      className="p-1 hover:bg-gray-700 rounded"
                      title="Pantalla completa"
                    >
                      <EyeIcon className="w-4 h-4 text-gray-400" />
                    </button>
                    
                    <button
                      onClick={deleteArtifact}
                      className="p-1 hover:bg-gray-700 rounded"
                      title="Eliminar"
                    >
                      <TrashIcon className="w-4 h-4 text-red-400" />
                    </button>
                  </div>
                </div>
                
                {/* Metadata */}
                <div className="flex items-center space-x-4 text-xs text-gray-500">
                  <span>Modelo: {selectedArtifact.metadata.model}</span>
                  <span>Tokens: {selectedArtifact.metadata.tokens}</span>
                  <span>Tama√±o: {(selectedArtifact.metadata.size / 1024).toFixed(1)}KB</span>
                  <span>Versi√≥n: {selectedArtifact.metadata.version}</span>
                </div>
              </div>
              
              {/* Preview content */}
              <div className="flex-1 overflow-hidden">
                {isEditing ? (
                  <div className="h-full flex flex-col">
                    <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-2 border-b border-gray-700">
                      <span className="text-sm text-gray-300">Editando</span>
                      <div className="flex space-x-2">
                        <button
                          onClick={saveEdit}
                          className="px-3 py-1 bg-green-600 hover:bg-green-700 text-white text-sm rounded transition-colors"
                        >
                          Guardar
                        </button>
                        <button
                          onClick={() => setIsEditing(false)}
                          className="px-3 py-1 bg-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-500 text-white text-sm rounded transition-colors"
                        >
                          Cancelar
                        </button>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <textarea
                      value={editedContent}
                      onChange={(e) => setEditedContent(e.target.value)}
                      className="flex-1 bg-gray-900 text-white p-4 font-mono text-sm resize-none focus:outline-none"
                    />
                  </div>
                ) : (
                  <div className={`h-full ${
                    viewMode === 'split' ? 'flex' : ''
                  }`}>
                    {/* Preview */}
                    {(viewMode === 'preview' || viewMode === 'split') && (
                      <div className={`${
                        viewMode === 'split' ? 'w-1/2 border-r border-gray-700' : 'w-full'
                      } overflow-auto`}>
                        {selectedArtifact.type === 'html' ? (
                          <iframe
                            ref={previewRef}
                            className="w-full h-full border-none"
                            sandbox="allow-scripts allow-same-origin"
                          />
                        ) : selectedArtifact.type === 'image' ? (
                          <div className="p-4">
                            <img 
                              src={selectedArtifact.content} 
                              alt={selectedArtifact.title}
                              className="max-w-full h-auto"
                            />
                          </div>
                        ) : selectedArtifact.type === 'video' ? (
                          <div className="p-4">
                            <video 
                              ref={videoRef}
                              controls 
                              className="w-full"
                              src={selectedArtifact.content}
                            />
                          </div>
                        ) : selectedArtifact.type === 'audio' ? (
                          <div className="p-4">
                            <audio 
                              ref={audioRef}
                              controls 
                              className="w-full"
                              src={selectedArtifact.content}
                            />
                          </div>
                        ) : (
                          <div className="p-4">
                            <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-4 text-gray-900">
                              <pre className="whitespace-pre-wrap text-sm">
                                {selectedArtifact.content}
                              </pre>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    )}
                    
                    {/* Code view */}
                    {(viewMode === 'code' || viewMode === 'split') && (
                      <div className={`${
                        viewMode === 'split' ? 'w-1/2' : 'w-full'
                      } overflow-auto`}>
                        <div className="bg-gray-900 h-full">
                          <pre className="p-4 text-sm text-gray-200 font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap">
                            {selectedArtifact.content}
                          </pre>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
              
              {/* Execution result */}
              {executionResult && (
                <div className={`p-2 border-t border-gray-700 ${
                  executionResult.success ? 'bg-green-900/20' : 'bg-red-900/20'
                }`}>
                  <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
                    {executionResult.success ? (
                      <CheckIcon className="w-4 h-4 text-green-400" />
                    ) : (
                      <XMarkIcon className="w-4 h-4 text-red-400" />
                    )}
                    <span className={`text-sm ${
                      executionResult.success ? 'text-green-400' : 'text-red-400'
                    }`}>
                      {executionResult.message}
                    </span>
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}
            </>
          ) : (
            <div className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center text-gray-500">
              <div className="text-center">
                <DocumentTextIcon className="w-16 h-16 mx-auto mb-4 opacity-50" />
                <p>Selecciona un artefacto para ver la vista previa</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
      
      {/* Fullscreen modal */}
      {showFullscreen && selectedArtifact && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-90 flex items-center justify-center z-50">
          <div className="w-full h-full max-w-7xl max-h-full p-4">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
              <h3 className="text-xl font-medium text-white">
                {selectedArtifact.title}
              </h3>
              <button
                onClick={() => setShowFullscreen(false)}
                className="text-white hover:text-gray-300"
              >
                <XMarkIcon className="w-6 h-6" />
              </button>
            </div>
            
            <div className="bg-gray-800 rounded-lg h-full overflow-auto">
              {selectedArtifact.type === 'html' ? (
                <iframe
                  className="w-full h-full border-none rounded-lg"
                  srcDoc={selectedArtifact.content}
                  sandbox="allow-scripts allow-same-origin"
                />
              ) : (
                <div className="p-4">
                  <pre className="text-white whitespace-pre-wrap text-sm">
                    {selectedArtifact.content}
                  </pre>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
      
      {/* Footer */}
      <div className="p-3 border-t border-gray-700">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-xs text-gray-500">
          <span>Modelo actual: {currentModel}</span>
          {selectedArtifact && (
            <span>
              {filteredArtifacts.findIndex(a => a.id === selectedArtifact.id) + 1} de {filteredArtifacts.length}
            </span>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default ArtifactPreview;

          
Ahora creo el archivo principal index.tsx para inicializar la aplicaci√≥n React.
        
            
toolName: write_to_file
            
status: success
          
            
filePath: C:\Users\Neizan\Desktop\Nexus_PowerUP\src\index.tsx
          
content: import React from 'react';
import ReactDOM from 'react-dom/client';
import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { ReactQueryDevtools } from '@tanstack/react-query-devtools';
import App from './App';
import './App.css';

// Configuraci√≥n de React Query
const queryClient = new QueryClient({
  defaultOptions: {
    queries: {
      staleTime: 5 * 60 * 1000, // 5 minutos
      cacheTime: 10 * 60 * 1000, // 10 minutos
      retry: 2,
      refetchOnWindowFocus: false,
    },
    mutations: {
      retry: 1,
    },
  },
});

// Configuraci√≥n de desarrollo
const isDevelopment = process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development';

// Error boundary para capturar errores de React
class ErrorBoundary extends React.Component<
  { children: React.ReactNode },
  { hasError: boolean; error?: Error }
> {
  constructor(props: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
    super(props);
    this.state = { hasError: false };
  }

  static getDerivedStateFromError(error: Error) {
    return { hasError: true, error };
  }

  componentDidCatch(error: Error, errorInfo: React.ErrorInfo) {
    console.error('Error capturado por ErrorBoundary:', error, errorInfo);
    
    // En producci√≥n, enviar error a servicio de monitoreo
    if (!isDevelopment) {
      // TODO: Integrar con servicio de monitoreo (Sentry, LogRocket, etc.)
    }
  }

  render() {
    if (this.state.hasError) {
      return (
        <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-900 flex items-center justify-center">
          <div className="text-center p-8">
            <div className="mb-4">
              <svg 
                className="w-16 h-16 text-red-500 mx-auto" 
                fill="none" 
                stroke="currentColor" 
                viewBox="0 0 24 24"
              >
                <path 
                  strokeLinecap="round" 
                  strokeLinejoin="round" 
                  strokeWidth={2} 
                  d="M12 9v2m0 4h.01m-6.938 4h13.856c1.54 0 2.502-1.667 1.732-2.5L13.732 4c-.77-.833-1.964-.833-2.732 0L3.732 16.5c-.77.833.192 2.5 1.732 2.5z" 
                />
              </svg>
            </div>
            <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white mb-2">
              ¬°Oops! Algo sali√≥ mal
            </h1>
            <p className="text-gray-400 mb-6">
              Ha ocurrido un error inesperado en NEXUS AI Studio.
            </p>
            {isDevelopment && this.state.error && (
              <details className="text-left bg-gray-800 p-4 rounded-lg mb-4">
                <summary className="text-red-400 cursor-pointer mb-2">
                  Detalles del error (desarrollo)
                </summary>
                <pre className="text-xs text-gray-300 overflow-auto">
                  {this.state.error.stack}
                </pre>
              </details>
            )}
            <div className="space-x-4">
              <button
                onClick={() => window.location.reload()}
                className="px-4 py-2 bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-700 text-white rounded-lg transition-colors"
              >
                Recargar Aplicaci√≥n
              </button>
              <button
                onClick={() => {
                  localStorage.clear();
                  window.location.reload();
                }}
                className="px-4 py-2 bg-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-700 text-white rounded-lg transition-colors"
              >
                Reiniciar Datos
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      );
    }

    return this.props.children;
  }
}

// Funci√≥n para verificar compatibilidad del navegador
const checkBrowserCompatibility = () => {
  const requiredFeatures = [
    'fetch',
    'Promise',
    'localStorage',
    'sessionStorage',
    'WebSocket'
  ];
  
  const missingFeatures = requiredFeatures.filter(feature => {
    return !(feature in window);
  });
  
  if (missingFeatures.length > 0) {
    console.warn('Caracter√≠sticas no soportadas:', missingFeatures);
    
    // Mostrar mensaje de compatibilidad
    const compatibilityMessage = document.createElement('div');
    compatibilityMessage.innerHTML = `
      <div style="
        position: fixed;
        top: 0;
        left: 0;
        width: 100%;
        height: 100%;
        background: #1f2937;
        color: white;
        display: flex;
        align-items: center;
        justify-content: center;
        z-index: 9999;
        font-family: system-ui, -apple-system, sans-serif;
      ">
        <div style="text-align: center; padding: 2rem;">
          <h1 style="font-size: 2rem; margin-bottom: 1rem;">Navegador No Compatible</h1>
          <p style="margin-bottom: 2rem; color: #9ca3af;">
            NEXUS AI Studio requiere un navegador m√°s moderno.
          </p>
          <p style="color: #9ca3af;">
            Por favor, actualiza tu navegador o usa Chrome, Firefox, Safari o Edge.
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
    document.body.appendChild(compatibilityMessage);
    return false;
  }
  
  return true;
};

// Funci√≥n para inicializar la aplicaci√≥n
const initializeApp = () => {
  // Verificar compatibilidad
  if (!checkBrowserCompatibility()) {
    return;
  }
  
  // Configurar variables globales para desarrollo
  if (isDevelopment) {
    // Exponer QueryClient para debugging
    (window as any).__NEXUS_QUERY_CLIENT__ = queryClient;
    
    // Logs de desarrollo
    console.log('üöÄ NEXUS AI Studio - Modo Desarrollo');
    console.log('üìä React Query Client:', queryClient);
    console.log('üé® Tailwind CSS cargado');
  }
  
  // Obtener el elemento root
  const rootElement = document.getElementById('root');
  if (!rootElement) {
    throw new Error('No se encontr√≥ el elemento root');
  }
  
  // Crear root de React 18
  const root = ReactDOM.createRoot(rootElement);
  
  // Renderizar la aplicaci√≥n
  root.render(
    <React.StrictMode>
      <ErrorBoundary>
        <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
          <App />
          {isDevelopment && (
            <ReactQueryDevtools 
              initialIsOpen={false} 
              position="bottom-right"
            />
          )}
        </QueryClientProvider>
      </ErrorBoundary>
    </React.StrictMode>
  );
  
  // Configurar service worker en producci√≥n
  if (!isDevelopment && 'serviceWorker' in navigator) {
    window.addEventListener('load', () => {
      navigator.serviceWorker.register('/sw.js')
        .then((registration) => {
          console.log('SW registrado: ', registration);
        })
        .catch((registrationError) => {
          console.log('SW fall√≥: ', registrationError);
        });
    });
  }
  
  // Configurar manejo de errores globales
  window.addEventListener('error', (event) => {
    console.error('Error global:', event.error);
    
    if (!isDevelopment) {
      // TODO: Enviar a servicio de monitoreo
    }
  });
  
  window.addEventListener('unhandledrejection', (event) => {
    console.error('Promise rechazada:', event.reason);
    
    if (!isDevelopment) {
      // TODO: Enviar a servicio de monitoreo
    }
  });
  
  // Configurar shortcuts globales
  document.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
    // Ctrl/Cmd + K para b√∫squeda r√°pida
    if ((event.ctrlKey || event.metaKey) && event.key === 'k') {
      event.preventDefault();
      // TODO: Abrir b√∫squeda r√°pida
      console.log('B√∫squeda r√°pida activada');
    }
    
    // Ctrl/Cmd + Shift + P para paleta de comandos
    if ((event.ctrlKey || event.metaKey) && event.shiftKey && event.key === 'P') {
      event.preventDefault();
      // TODO: Abrir paleta de comandos
      console.log('Paleta de comandos activada');
    }
    
    // F11 para pantalla completa
    if (event.key === 'F11') {
      event.preventDefault();
      if (document.fullscreenElement) {
        document.exitFullscreen();
      } else {
        document.documentElement.requestFullscreen();
      }
    }
  });
  
  // Configurar tema inicial
  const savedTheme = localStorage.getItem('nexus-theme');
  if (savedTheme) {
    document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', savedTheme);
  } else {
    // Detectar preferencia del sistema
    const prefersDark = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
    document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', prefersDark ? 'dark' : 'light');
  }
  
  // Escuchar cambios en la preferencia del sistema
  window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').addEventListener('change', (e) => {
    if (!localStorage.getItem('nexus-theme')) {
      document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', e.matches ? 'dark' : 'light');
    }
  });
  
  // Configurar analytics en producci√≥n
  if (!isDevelopment) {
    // TODO: Inicializar analytics (Google Analytics, Mixpanel, etc.)
  }
  
  // Mostrar informaci√≥n de la aplicaci√≥n
  console.log(`
üéØ NEXUS AI Studio v1.0.0
üîß Entorno: ${isDevelopment ? 'Desarrollo' : 'Producci√≥n'}
‚öõÔ∏è  React: ${React.version}
üé® Tailwind CSS: Cargado
üîÑ React Query: Configurado
`);
};

// Inicializar cuando el DOM est√© listo
if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initializeApp);
} else {
  initializeApp();
}

// Exportar para testing
export { queryClient };

toolName: write_to_file
            
status: success
          
            
filePath: C:\Users\Neizan\Desktop\Nexus_PowerUP\.husky\pre-commit
          
content: #!/usr/bin/env sh
. "$(dirname -- "$0")/_/husky.sh"

# NEXUS AI Studio - Pre-commit Hook
# =============================================================================
# This hook runs before each commit to ensure code quality

echo "üîç Running pre-commit checks..."

# Run lint-staged to check only staged files
npx lint-staged

# Check if lint-staged passed
if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
  echo "‚ùå Pre-commit checks failed. Please fix the issues and try again."
  exit 1
fi

# Run type checking
echo "üîç Running TypeScript type checking..."
npm run type-check

if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
  echo "‚ùå TypeScript type checking failed. Please fix the type errors and try again."
  exit 1
fi

# Run tests on staged files (optional)
echo "üß™ Running tests on staged files..."
npm run test:staged

if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
  echo "‚ùå Tests failed. Please fix the failing tests and try again."
  exit 1
fi

echo "‚úÖ All pre-commit checks passed!"

          
Ahora creo el archivo de configuraci√≥n de Husky para el hook pre-push.
        
            
toolName: write_to_file
            
status: success
          
            
filePath: C:\Users\Neizan\Desktop\Nexus_PowerUP\.husky\pre-push
          
content: #!/usr/bin/env sh
. "$(dirname -- "$0")/_/husky.sh"

# NEXUS AI Studio - Pre-push Hook
# =============================================================================
# This hook runs before each push to ensure code quality and build success

echo "üöÄ Running pre-push checks..."

# Get the current branch name
branch=$(git rev-parse --abbrev-ref HEAD)

# Prevent pushing to main/master branch directly (optional)
if [ "$branch" = "main" ] || [ "$branch" = "master" ]; then
  echo "‚ö†Ô∏è  Warning: You are about to push to the $branch branch."
  echo "Please make sure this is intentional and you have proper authorization."
  read -p "Do you want to continue? (y/N): " -n 1 -r
  echo
  if [[ ! $REPLY =~ ^[Yy]$ ]]; then
    echo "‚ùå Push cancelled."
    exit 1
  fi
fi

# Run full linting
echo "üîç Running ESLint..."
npm run lint

if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
  echo "‚ùå ESLint failed. Please fix the linting errors and try again."
  exit 1
fi

# Run Stylelint
echo "üé® Running Stylelint..."
npm run lint:css

if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
  echo "‚ùå Stylelint failed. Please fix the CSS linting errors and try again."
  exit 1
fi

# Run TypeScript type checking
echo "üîç Running TypeScript type checking..."
npm run type-check

if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
  echo "‚ùå TypeScript type checking failed. Please fix the type errors and try again."
  exit 1
fi

# Run all tests
echo "üß™ Running all tests..."
npm run test:ci

if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
  echo "‚ùå Tests failed. Please fix the failing tests and try again."
  exit 1
fi

# Run build to ensure everything compiles
echo "üèóÔ∏è  Running build..."
npm run build

if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
  echo "‚ùå Build failed. Please fix the build errors and try again."
  exit 1
fi

# Check bundle size (optional)
echo "üì¶ Checking bundle size..."
npm run analyze:bundle

if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
  echo "‚ö†Ô∏è  Bundle analysis failed, but continuing with push."
fi

# Security audit (optional)
echo "üîí Running security audit..."
npm audit --audit-level moderate

if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
  echo "‚ö†Ô∏è  Security vulnerabilities found. Consider running 'npm audit fix'."
  echo "Continuing with push, but please address these issues soon."
fi

echo "‚úÖ All pre-push checks passed! üéâ"
echo "üì§ Pushing to $branch..."

          
Ahora creo el archivo de configuraci√≥n de Husky para el hook commit-msg.
        
            
toolName: write_to_file
            
status: success
          
            
filePath: C:\Users\Neizan\Desktop\Nexus_PowerUP\.husky\commit-msg
          
content: #!/usr/bin/env sh
. "$(dirname -- "$0")/_/husky.sh"

# NEXUS AI Studio - Commit Message Hook
# =============================================================================
# This hook validates commit messages to ensure they follow conventional commits

echo "üìù Validating commit message..."

# Run commitlint to validate the commit message
npx --no-install commitlint --edit "$1"

if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
  echo "‚ùå Commit message validation failed."
  echo ""
  echo "Please follow the conventional commit format:"
  echo "  <type>[optional scope]: <description>"
  echo ""
  echo "Examples:"
  echo "  feat: add new AI model integration"
  echo "  fix: resolve memory leak in file processor"
  echo "  docs: update installation guide"
  echo "  style: format code with prettier"
  echo "  refactor: restructure component hierarchy"
  echo "  test: add unit tests for utility functions"
  echo "  chore: update dependencies"
  echo ""
  echo "Types: feat, fix, docs, style, refactor, test, chore, perf, ci, build, revert"
  echo "Scopes (optional): ui, api, core, electron, ai, storage, auth, etc."
  echo ""
  exit 1
fi

echo "‚úÖ Commit message is valid!"

content: module.exports = {
  extends: ['@commitlint/config-conventional'],
  rules: {
    // Type enum
    'type-enum': [
      2,
      'always',
      [
        'feat',     // New feature
        'fix',      // Bug fix
        'docs',     // Documentation changes
        'style',    // Code style changes (formatting, etc.)
        'refactor', // Code refactoring
        'test',     // Adding or updating tests
        'chore',    // Maintenance tasks
        'perf',     // Performance improvements
        'ci',       // CI/CD changes
        'build',    // Build system changes
        'revert',   // Revert previous commit
        'wip',      // Work in progress (use sparingly)
        'hotfix',   // Critical bug fixes
        'release',  // Release commits
        'merge',    // Merge commits
      ],
    ],
    
    // Scope enum (optional but recommended)
    'scope-enum': [
      2,
      'always',
      [
        // Core areas
        'core',
        'api',
        'ui',
        'ux',
        
        // Features
        'ai',
        'chat',
        'editor',
        'file-explorer',
        'project-manager',
        'artifact-preview',
        'code-generation',

        // Infrastructure

        'docker',

        'backup',
        
        // Documentation

        'changelog',
        'contributing',

        'user-guide',
        
        // Dependencies
        'deps',
        'dev-deps',
        'peer-deps',
        
        // Configuration
        'config',
        'env',
        'scripts',
        'workflows',

        // Misc
        'assets',
        'icons',
        'fonts',

        'types',

        'services',
        'hooks',
        'contexts',
        'providers',
        'store',
        'reducers',
        'actions',
        'selectors',
        'middleware',
      ],
    ],
    
    // Case rules
    'type-case': [2, 'always', 'lower-case'],
    'scope-case': [2, 'always', 'lower-case'],
    'subject-case': [2, 'always', 'lower-case'],
    
    // Empty rules
    'type-empty': [2, 'never'],
    'subject-empty': [2, 'never'],
    
    // Length rules
    'header-max-length': [2, 'always', 100],
    'subject-max-length': [2, 'always', 80],
    'body-max-line-length': [2, 'always', 100],
    'footer-max-line-length': [2, 'always', 100],
    
    // Format rules
    'header-full-stop': [2, 'never', '.'],
    'subject-full-stop': [2, 'never', '.'],
    
    // Body and footer rules
    'body-leading-blank': [2, 'always'],
    'footer-leading-blank': [2, 'always'],
    
    // Scope rules
    'scope-empty': [0, 'never'], // Allow empty scope
    
    // Custom rules for better commit messages
    'subject-min-length': [2, 'always', 10],
    'type-max-length': [2, 'always', 10],
    'scope-max-length': [2, 'always', 20],
  ],
  
  // Custom prompt configuration
  prompt: {
    questions: {
      type: {
        description: 'Select the type of change that you\'re committing:',
        enum: {
          feat: {
            description: 'A new feature',
            title: 'Features',
            emoji: '‚ú®',
          },
          fix: {
            description: 'A bug fix',
            title: 'Bug Fixes',
            emoji: 'üêõ',
          },
          docs: {
            description: 'Documentation only changes',
            title: 'Documentation',
            emoji: 'üìö',
          },
          style: {
            description: 'Changes that do not affect the meaning of the code',
            title: 'Styles',
            emoji: 'üíé',
          },
          refactor: {
            description: 'A code change that neither fixes a bug nor adds a feature',
            title: 'Code Refactoring',
            emoji: 'üì¶',
          },
          perf: {
            description: 'A code change that improves performance',
            title: 'Performance Improvements',
            emoji: 'üöÄ',
          },
          test: {

            title: 'Tests',
            emoji: 'üö®',
          },
          build: {
            description: 'Changes that affect the build system or external dependencies',
            title: 'Builds',
            emoji: 'üõ†',
          },
          ci: {
            description: 'Changes to our CI configuration files and scripts',
            title: 'Continuous Integrations',
            emoji: '‚öôÔ∏è',
          },
          chore: {
            description: 'Other changes that don\'t modify src or test files',
            title: 'Chores',
            emoji: '‚ôªÔ∏è',
          },
          revert: {
            description: 'Reverts a previous commit',
            title: 'Reverts',
            emoji: 'üóë',
          },
        },
      },
      scope: {
        description: 'What is the scope of this change (e.g. component or file name)',
      },
      subject: {
        description: 'Write a short, imperative tense description of the change',
      },
      body: {
        description: 'Provide a longer description of the change',
      },
      isBreaking: {
        description: 'Are there any breaking changes?',
      },
      breakingBody: {
        description: 'A BREAKING CHANGE commit requires a body. Please enter a longer description of the commit itself',
      },
      breaking: {
        description: 'Describe the breaking changes',
      },
      isIssueAffected: {
        description: 'Does this change affect any open issues?',
      },
      issuesBody: {
        description: 'If issues are closed, the commit requires a body. Please enter a longer description of the commit itself',
      },
      issues: {
        description: 'Add issue references (e.g. "fix #123", "re #123".)',
      },
    },
  },
  
  // Help URL
  helpUrl: 'https://github.com/conventional-changelog/commitlint/#what-is-commitlint',
  
  // Default ignore patterns
  ignores: [
    (commit) => commit.includes('WIP'),
    (commit) => commit.includes('wip'),
    (commit) => commit.includes('Merge'),
    (commit) => commit.includes('merge'),
  ],
  
  // Default rules to disable
  defaultIgnores: true,
};

    "npm run lint:package",
    "git add"
  ],

    "bash -c 'npm run type-check'"
  ],
  "src/**/*.{test,spec}.{js,jsx,ts,tsx}": [
    "npm run test:staged"
  ],
  "*.{js,jsx,ts,tsx,css,scss,sass,less,json,md,mdx,yml,yaml,html,htm}": [

content: import type { StorybookConfig } from '@storybook/react-vite';
import { mergeConfig } from 'vite';
import path from 'path';

const config: StorybookConfig = {
  stories: [
    '../src/**/*.stories.@(js|jsx|ts|tsx|mdx)',
    '../src/**/*.story.@(js|jsx|ts|tsx|mdx)',
    '../stories/**/*.stories.@(js|jsx|ts|tsx|mdx)',
    '../stories/**/*.story.@(js|jsx|ts|tsx|mdx)',
  ],
  
  addons: [
    '@storybook/addon-links',
    '@storybook/addon-essentials',
    '@storybook/addon-interactions',
    '@storybook/addon-docs',
    '@storybook/addon-controls',
    '@storybook/addon-actions',
    '@storybook/addon-viewport',
    '@storybook/addon-backgrounds',
    '@storybook/addon-toolbars',
    '@storybook/addon-measure',
    '@storybook/addon-outline',
    '@storybook/addon-a11y',
    '@storybook/addon-design-tokens',
    '@storybook/addon-storysource',
    'storybook-dark-mode',
    '@storybook/addon-jest',
    '@chromatic-com/storybook',
  ],
  
  framework: {
    name: '@storybook/react-vite',
    options: {},
  },
  
  typescript: {
    check: false,
    reactDocgen: 'react-docgen-typescript',
    reactDocgenTypescriptOptions: {
      shouldExtractLiteralValuesFromEnum: true,
      propFilter: (prop) => (prop.parent ? !/node_modules/.test(prop.parent.fileName) : true),
      compilerOptions: {
        allowSyntheticDefaultImports: false,
        esModuleInterop: false,
      },
    },
  },
  
  docs: {
    autodocs: 'tag',
    defaultName: 'Documentation',
  },
  
  viteFinal: async (config) => {
    return mergeConfig(config, {
      resolve: {
        alias: {
          '@': path.resolve(__dirname, '../src'),
          '@/components': path.resolve(__dirname, '../src/components'),
          '@/contexts': path.resolve(__dirname, '../src/contexts'),
          '@/hooks': path.resolve(__dirname, '../src/hooks'),
          '@/utils': path.resolve(__dirname, '../src/utils'),
          '@/types': path.resolve(__dirname, '../src/types'),
          '@/lib': path.resolve(__dirname, '../src/lib'),
          '@/assets': path.resolve(__dirname, '../src/assets'),
          '@/styles': path.resolve(__dirname, '../src/styles'),
          '@/config': path.resolve(__dirname, '../src/config'),
          '@/services': path.resolve(__dirname, '../src/services'),
          '@/store': path.resolve(__dirname, '../src/store'),
        },
      },
      define: {
        global: 'globalThis',
        __STORYBOOK__: true,
      },
      css: {
        postcss: {
          plugins: [
            require('tailwindcss'),
            require('autoprefixer'),
          ],
        },
      },
      optimizeDeps: {
        include: [
          '@storybook/react',
          '@storybook/addon-docs',
          '@radix-ui/react-icons',
          '@heroicons/react/24/outline',
          '@heroicons/react/24/solid',
          'react',
          'react-dom',
          'react-router-dom',
        ],
      },
    });
  },
  
  core: {
    disableTelemetry: true,
  },
  
  features: {
    buildStoriesJson: true,
    storyStoreV7: true,
  },
  
  staticDirs: [
    '../public',
    '../src/assets',
  ],
  
  env: (config) => ({
    ...config,
    STORYBOOK: 'true',
  }),
  
  refs: {
    'design-system': {
      title: 'NEXUS Design System',
      url: 'https://nexus-design-system.netlify.app',
      expanded: false,
    },
  },
  
  managerHead: (head) => `
    ${head}
    <link rel="icon" type="image/svg+xml" href="/favicon.svg" />
    <title>NEXUS AI Studio - Storybook</title>
    <meta name="description" content="Component library and design system for NEXUS AI Studio" />
  `,
  
  previewHead: (head) => `
    ${head}
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@100;200;300;400;500;600;700;800;900&family=JetBrains+Mono:ital,wght@0,100;0,200;0,300;0,400;0,500;0,600;0,700;0,800;1,100;1,200;1,300;1,400;1,500;1,600;1,700;1,800&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
    <style>
      body {
        font-family: 'Inter', -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', 'Roboto', 'Oxygen', 'Ubuntu', 'Cantarell', 'Fira Sans', 'Droid Sans', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;
      }
      
      code, pre {
        font-family: 'JetBrains Mono', 'Fira Code', 'Monaco', 'Consolas', 'Ubuntu Mono', monospace;
      }
    </style>
  `,
};

      // Apply theme class to body
      document.body.className = `${theme} density-${density}`;
      
      // Set locale attribute
      document.documentElement.lang = locale;
      
      return (
        <div className={`storybook-wrapper theme-${theme} density-${density}`}>
          <Story />
        </div>
      );

Ahora creo el archivo de configuraci√≥n de Docker para el desarrollo y producci√≥n.
        
            
toolName: write_to_file
            
status: success
          
            
filePath: C:\Users\Neizan\Desktop\Nexus_PowerUP\Dockerfile
          
content: # NEXUS AI Studio - Multi-stage Dockerfile
# =============================================================================
# This Dockerfile creates optimized images for development and production

# Base image with Node.js
FROM node:18-alpine AS base

# Install system dependencies
RUN apk add --no-cache \
    git \
    python3 \
    make \
    g++ \
    cairo-dev \
    jpeg-dev \
    pango-dev \
    musl-dev \
    giflib-dev \
    pixman-dev \
    pangomm-dev \
    libjpeg-turbo-dev \
    freetype-dev

# Set working directory
WORKDIR /app

# Copy package files
COPY package*.json ./
COPY pnpm-lock.yaml* ./

# Install pnpm
RUN npm install -g pnpm@latest

# Development stage
FROM base AS development

# Install all dependencies (including dev dependencies)
RUN pnpm install --frozen-lockfile

# Copy source code
COPY . .

# Expose development port
EXPOSE 3000
EXPOSE 51204
EXPOSE 6006

# Development command
CMD ["pnpm", "dev"]

# Build stage
FROM base AS builder

# Install all dependencies
RUN pnpm install --frozen-lockfile

# Copy source code
COPY . .

# Set environment variables for build
ENV NODE_ENV=production
ENV GENERATE_SOURCEMAP=false
ENV INLINE_RUNTIME_CHUNK=false

# Build the application
RUN pnpm build

# Production stage
FROM nginx:alpine AS production

# Install Node.js for SSR (if needed)
RUN apk add --no-cache nodejs npm

# Copy built application
COPY --from=builder /app/dist /usr/share/nginx/html

# Copy nginx configuration
COPY docker/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf
COPY docker/default.conf /etc/nginx/conf.d/default.conf

# Copy SSL certificates (if available)
# COPY docker/ssl/ /etc/nginx/ssl/

# Create nginx user and set permissions
RUN addgroup -g 1001 -S nginx && \
    adduser -S nginx -u 1001 -G nginx && \
    chown -R nginx:nginx /usr/share/nginx/html && \
    chown -R nginx:nginx /var/cache/nginx && \
    chown -R nginx:nginx /var/log/nginx && \
    chown -R nginx:nginx /etc/nginx/conf.d

# Switch to non-root user
USER nginx

# Expose port
EXPOSE 80
EXPOSE 443

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \
    CMD curl -f http://localhost/ || exit 1

# Start nginx
CMD ["nginx", "-g", "daemon off;"]

# Storybook stage
FROM base AS storybook

# Install dependencies
RUN pnpm install --frozen-lockfile

# Copy source code
COPY . .

# Build Storybook
RUN pnpm build-storybook

# Serve Storybook
FROM nginx:alpine AS storybook-serve

# Copy Storybook build
COPY --from=storybook /app/storybook-static /usr/share/nginx/html

# Copy nginx configuration for Storybook
COPY docker/storybook-nginx.conf /etc/nginx/conf.d/default.conf

# Expose port
EXPOSE 80

# Start nginx
CMD ["nginx", "-g", "daemon off;"]

# Testing stage
FROM base AS testing

# Install dependencies
RUN pnpm install --frozen-lockfile

# Copy source code
COPY . .

# Install additional testing dependencies
RUN apk add --no-cache \
    chromium \
    nss \
    freetype \
    freetype-dev \
    harfbuzz \
    ca-certificates \
    ttf-freefont

# Set Puppeteer to use installed Chromium
ENV PUPPETEER_SKIP_CHROMIUM_DOWNLOAD=true
ENV PUPPETEER_EXECUTABLE_PATH=/usr/bin/chromium-browser

# Run tests
CMD ["pnpm", "test:ci"]

# Electron build stage
FROM base AS electron-builder

# Install additional dependencies for Electron
RUN apk add --no-cache \
    wine \
    xvfb \
    fakeroot \
    dpkg \
    rpm \
    zip \
    unzip

# Install dependencies
RUN pnpm install --frozen-lockfile

# Copy source code
COPY . .

# Build web application first
RUN pnpm build

# Build Electron application
RUN pnpm electron:build

# Copy built Electron apps
FROM alpine:latest AS electron-dist

# Copy Electron builds
COPY --from=electron-builder /app/electron-dist /electron-dist

# Create volume for output
VOLUME ["/output"]

# Copy builds to output
CMD cp -r /electron-dist/* /output/

# Multi-platform build stage
FROM --platform=$BUILDPLATFORM base AS multi-platform

ARG TARGETPLATFORM
ARG BUILDPLATFORM

# Install dependencies based on platform
RUN if [ "$TARGETPLATFORM" = "linux/amd64" ]; then \
        echo "Building for AMD64"; \
    elif [ "$TARGETPLATFORM" = "linux/arm64" ]; then \
        echo "Building for ARM64"; \
    elif [ "$TARGETPLATFORM" = "linux/arm/v7" ]; then \
        echo "Building for ARMv7"; \
    fi

# Install dependencies
RUN pnpm install --frozen-lockfile

# Copy source code
COPY . .

# Build application
RUN pnpm build

# Final production image
FROM nginx:alpine AS final

# Copy built application
COPY --from=multi-platform /app/dist /usr/share/nginx/html

# Copy nginx configuration
COPY docker/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf
COPY docker/default.conf /etc/nginx/conf.d/default.conf

# Set up security headers
RUN echo 'add_header X-Frame-Options "SAMEORIGIN" always;' >> /etc/nginx/conf.d/security.conf && \
    echo 'add_header X-Content-Type-Options "nosniff" always;' >> /etc/nginx/conf.d/security.conf && \
    echo 'add_header X-XSS-Protection "1; mode=block" always;' >> /etc/nginx/conf.d/security.conf && \
    echo 'add_header Referrer-Policy "strict-origin-when-cross-origin" always;' >> /etc/nginx/conf.d/security.conf

# Create non-root user
RUN addgroup -g 1001 -S nexus && \
    adduser -S nexus -u 1001 -G nexus

# Set ownership
RUN chown -R nexus:nexus /usr/share/nginx/html

# Switch to non-root user
USER nexus

# Expose port
EXPOSE 80

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \
    CMD wget --no-verbose --tries=1 --spider http://localhost/ || exit 1

# Start nginx
CMD ["nginx", "-g", "daemon off;"]

# Labels for metadata
LABEL maintainer="NEXUS AI Studio Team <team@nexus-ai-studio.com>"
LABEL version="1.0.0"
LABEL description="NEXUS AI Studio - Advanced AI-powered development environment"
LABEL org.opencontainers.image.title="NEXUS AI Studio"
LABEL org.opencontainers.image.description="Advanced AI-powered development environment"
LABEL org.opencontainers.image.version="1.0.0"
LABEL org.opencontainers.image.vendor="NEXUS AI Studio"
LABEL org.opencontainers.image.licenses="MIT"
LABEL org.opencontainers.image.source="https://github.com/nexus-ai-studio/nexus-powerup"
LABEL org.opencontainers.image.documentation="https://docs.nexus-ai-studio.com"

          
Ahora creo el archivo docker-compose.yml para orquestar los servicios de desarrollo.
        
            
toolName: write_to_file
            
status: success
          
            
filePath: C:\Users\Neizan\Desktop\Nexus_PowerUP\docker-compose.yml
          
content: # NEXUS AI Studio - Docker Compose Configuration
# =============================================================================
# This file defines the multi-service architecture for development and production

version: '3.8'

services:
  # Main application (development)
  app:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
      target: development
    container_name: nexus-app-dev
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"    # Vite dev server
      - "51204:51204"  # Vitest UI
    volumes:
      - .:/app
      - /app/node_modules
      - nexus-cache:/app/.cache
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=development
      - VITE_API_URL=http://localhost:3001
      - VITE_WS_URL=ws://localhost:3001
      - CHOKIDAR_USEPOLLING=true
    networks:
      - nexus-network
    depends_on:
      - api
      - redis
    restart: unless-stopped
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s

  # API Backend
  api:
    build:
      context: ./api
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    container_name: nexus-api
    ports:
      - "3001:3001"
    volumes:
      - ./api:/app
      - /app/node_modules
      - nexus-uploads:/app/uploads
      - nexus-storage:/app/storage
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=development
      - PORT=3001
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://nexus:nexus_password@postgres:5432/nexus_db
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379
      - JWT_SECRET=your-super-secret-jwt-key-change-in-production
      - OPENAI_API_KEY=${OPENAI_API_KEY}
      - ANTHROPIC_API_KEY=${ANTHROPIC_API_KEY}
      - GOOGLE_API_KEY=${GOOGLE_API_KEY}
      - DEEPSEEK_API_KEY=${DEEPSEEK_API_KEY}
    networks:
      - nexus-network
    depends_on:
      - postgres
      - redis
    restart: unless-stopped
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3001/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s

  # PostgreSQL Database
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    container_name: nexus-postgres
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    volumes:
      - nexus-postgres-data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./docker/postgres/init.sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init.sql
    environment:
      - POSTGRES_DB=nexus_db
      - POSTGRES_USER=nexus
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=nexus_password
      - POSTGRES_INITDB_ARGS=--encoding=UTF-8 --lc-collate=C --lc-ctype=C
    networks:
      - nexus-network
    restart: unless-stopped
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U nexus -d nexus_db"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s

  # Redis Cache
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: nexus-redis
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    volumes:
      - nexus-redis-data:/data
      - ./docker/redis/redis.conf:/usr/local/etc/redis/redis.conf
    command: redis-server /usr/local/etc/redis/redis.conf
    networks:
      - nexus-network
    restart: unless-stopped
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s

  # Nginx Reverse Proxy
  nginx:
    image: nginx:alpine
    container_name: nexus-nginx
    ports:
      - "80:80"
      - "443:443"
    volumes:
      - ./docker/nginx/nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf
      - ./docker/nginx/default.conf:/etc/nginx/conf.d/default.conf
      - ./docker/ssl:/etc/nginx/ssl
      - nexus-static:/usr/share/nginx/html
    networks:
      - nexus-network
    depends_on:
      - app
      - api
    restart: unless-stopped
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s

  # Storybook
  storybook:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
      target: storybook-serve
    container_name: nexus-storybook
    ports:
      - "6006:80"
    networks:
      - nexus-network
    restart: unless-stopped
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s

  # Elasticsearch (for search functionality)
  elasticsearch:
    image: docker.elastic.co/elasticsearch/elasticsearch:8.11.0
    container_name: nexus-elasticsearch
    ports:
      - "9200:9200"
      - "9300:9300"
    volumes:
      - nexus-elasticsearch-data:/usr/share/elasticsearch/data
    environment:
      - discovery.type=single-node
      - xpack.security.enabled=false
      - "ES_JAVA_OPTS=-Xms512m -Xmx512m"
    networks:
      - nexus-network
    restart: unless-stopped
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "curl -f http://localhost:9200/_cluster/health || exit 1"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 60s

  # MinIO (S3-compatible object storage)
  minio:
    image: minio/minio:latest
    container_name: nexus-minio
    ports:
      - "9000:9000"
      - "9001:9001"
    volumes:
      - nexus-minio-data:/data
    environment:
      - MINIO_ROOT_USER=nexus
      - MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD=nexus_minio_password
      - MINIO_BROWSER_REDIRECT_URL=http://localhost:9001
    command: server /data --console-address ":9001"
    networks:
      - nexus-network
    restart: unless-stopped
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:9000/minio/health/live"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s

  # Monitoring with Prometheus
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    container_name: nexus-prometheus
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"
    volumes:
      - ./docker/prometheus/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
      - nexus-prometheus-data:/prometheus
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml'
      - '--storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus'
      - '--web.console.libraries=/etc/prometheus/console_libraries'
      - '--web.console.templates=/etc/prometheus/consoles'
      - '--storage.tsdb.retention.time=200h'
      - '--web.enable-lifecycle'
    networks:
      - nexus-network
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Grafana for metrics visualization
  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    container_name: nexus-grafana
    ports:
      - "3002:3000"
    volumes:
      - nexus-grafana-data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ./docker/grafana/provisioning:/etc/grafana/provisioning
    environment:
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_USER=admin
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=nexus_grafana_password
      - GF_USERS_ALLOW_SIGN_UP=false
    networks:
      - nexus-network
    depends_on:
      - prometheus
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Jaeger for distributed tracing
  jaeger:
    image: jaegertracing/all-in-one:latest
    container_name: nexus-jaeger
    ports:
      - "16686:16686"
      - "14268:14268"
    environment:
      - COLLECTOR_OTLP_ENABLED=true
    networks:
      - nexus-network
    restart: unless-stopped

# Networks
networks:
  nexus-network:
    driver: bridge
    ipam:
      config:
        - subnet: 172.20.0.0/16

# Volumes
volumes:
  nexus-postgres-data:
    driver: local
  nexus-redis-data:
    driver: local
  nexus-elasticsearch-data:
    driver: local
  nexus-minio-data:
    driver: local
  nexus-prometheus-data:
    driver: local
  nexus-grafana-data:
    driver: local
  nexus-cache:
    driver: local
  nexus-uploads:
    driver: local
  nexus-storage:
    driver: local
  nexus-static:
    driver: local

content: import React from 'react';
import { Toaster as HotToaster } from 'react-hot-toast';

/**
 * Componente Toaster para mostrar notificaciones toast
 * Utiliza react-hot-toast como base
 */
export const Toaster: React.FC = () => {
  return (
    <HotToaster
      position="top-right"
      reverseOrder={false}
      gutter={8}
      containerClassName=""
      containerStyle={{}}
      toastOptions={{
        // Configuraci√≥n por defecto
        duration: 4000,
        style: {
          background: '#1f2937', // gray-800
          color: '#f9fafb', // gray-50
          border: '1px solid #374151', // gray-700
          borderRadius: '8px',
          fontSize: '14px',
          fontWeight: '500',
          padding: '12px 16px',
          boxShadow: '0 10px 15px -3px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 4px 6px -2px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)',
        },
        // Configuraci√≥n para toast de √©xito
        success: {
          duration: 3000,
          style: {
            background: '#065f46', // emerald-800
            border: '1px solid #10b981', // emerald-500
          },
          iconTheme: {
            primary: '#10b981', // emerald-500
            secondary: '#065f46', // emerald-800
          },
        },
        // Configuraci√≥n para toast de error
        error: {
          duration: 5000,
          style: {
            background: '#7f1d1d', // red-800
            border: '1px solid #ef4444', // red-500
          },
          iconTheme: {
            primary: '#ef4444', // red-500
            secondary: '#7f1d1d', // red-800
          },
        },
        // Configuraci√≥n para toast de loading
        loading: {
          style: {
            background: '#1e40af', // blue-800
            border: '1px solid #3b82f6', // blue-500
          },
          iconTheme: {
            primary: '#3b82f6', // blue-500
            secondary: '#1e40af', // blue-800
          },
        },
      }}
    />
  );
};

export default Toaster;
